Ghats (gootis) n. labo silsiladood oo buuro ah kala marana bartahama iyo koofurta Hindiya. Loona yaqaan the East ern Ghats and the Western Ghats.

ghee (gii) n. subag sixin ah oo laga shiilay caano lo’aad. ghetto (‘gedhaw) n., pl. ghettos or ghettoes. 1 xaafado hoose ama burbursan oo ka mid ah magaalooyinka Yurubta oo lagu khasbi jiray Yuhuuddu in ay dagto. 2 xaafad ama meel kasta oo gooni loo faquuqo ayada iyo dadka ku nool.

-v., -toed, -toing. faquuqid; gooni u dajin xaafado xun. e.g. Many refugees are put in isolated and ghettoed area. ghettoize (‘gedhaw,aayz) v. dejin meelo faquuqan ama bulsho gooni u takooran. e.g. Refugees and minority groups are ghettoized and have no opportunities. - ghettoization n.

ghost (goosti) n. naf; ruux ama rooxaan. e.g. The ghost of young boy haunted the building.

-give up the ghost, a naf-waayid. b bakhtin, siiba matoor.

ghostbuster (‘gawsti,bastar) n. [informal] 1 dad saara rooxaan. 2 qof barta awoodaha maskaxda ka baxsan (parapsychology), sida dad meelo kala fog jooga oo war ama wax kale isku tabiya (telepathy). 3 baare xisaab xil-ma-leh.

ghostly (‘gawstali) adj. ghostlier, ghostliest. la xiriira rooxaan arag ama maqal ahaan. e.g. A ghostly figure walked across the street. -ghostliness n.

ghost story n. sheeko baqdin leh oo ka hadasha rooxaan iyo dad dhintay oo la arkay ruuxooda.

ghost town n. tuulo laga qaxay; magaalo dadkii deganaan jiray ka wada guureen ama dad aad u tiro yar ku hareen. ghost word n. eray aan la adeegsan laakiin ku qoran qaamuusyada ama diiwaanada kale.

ghostwriter (‘gawsti,raaydhar) n. qof shaqadiisu tahay in uu wax u qoro dadka kale oo ayagu isku magacaabaan qoraaga. -ghostwrite v.

ghoul (guul) n. 1 balaayo, siiba mid qufata xabaalo oo quudata mayd. 2 qof ka hela dhimashada, burburka, iyo aafooyinka. -ghoulish adj.; -ghoulishly adv.; -ghoul ishness n.

giant (‘jaaynti) n. 1 qof la mala-awaalay oo aad uga wayn ugana xoog badan dadka. 2 qof, xoolo, ama geed aad u wayn. 3 shirkad ama urur ballaaran.

-go on, a socotin; wadid. e.g. We can’t go on fighting for nothing. b hadlid in badan, siiba xanaaq ku jiro. c sii hadlid ama sii samayn wax hakadgalay. e.g. After a long pause she went on talking. d [informal] dalqamin; hadal ka sii raadin. e.g. Go on, tell me more!

Honda (‘haandha), Soichiro (1906-92), nin Japanese ah oo leh warshad samaysa baabuur: 1934, ayuu furay warshaddii kowaad oo mootooyin samaysa, 1960 wuxuu u baddalay mid baabuur samaysa.

-n. liif ama dhagax-sulubeed lagu soofeeyo mandiilo. honest (‘aanisti) adj. 1 daacad ama mukhlis ah; qumman ama aamin ah. e.g. She was an honest person. 2 kasbada ama shaqaysta xoolo xaq ah. e.g. He is fighting to make an honest living.

honk (haangk; howngk) n. 1 dhawaqa boola-boola duur joog ah. 2 dhawaq daran ee hoon gaari.

-v. dhawaajin hoon (horn) gaari. e.g. Taxi driver honked as he drove by our store.

honky (‘haangki; ‘hoongki) n., pl. -ies. [informal] hadal qadaf ah oo dadka madaw ugu yeeraan qof cad ama dhammaan caddaanka.

Honolulu (,haanal’uuluu) magala madaxda gobolka Hawaii. honor (‘aanar) n. 1 xushmo; ikraam. e.g. He won honor for inventing telephone. He was a man of honor. 2 qof sharaf u soo hooya kuwa kale. e.g. Our leader is an honor to Somalia. 3 qaddarin iyo xushmo-sare. e.g. Ahmed-gurey is an honor to our country. 4 qaadasho; aqbalyo. e.g. This restaurant doesn’t honor credit cards. 5 sharaf. e.g. It’s an honor to meet you.

-do the honors, [informal] qabatin hawl bulsho ama xafalad.

-in honor of, xushmo.

-one one’s honor, xil saaran qof. e.g. They are their honor as Muslims not to steal.

-there’s honor among thieves, [maah-maah] tuugooyin xad xira oo ay xushmeeyaan baa jira. honorable (‘aanarabal) adj. 1 keena ama istaahila sharaf. e.g. An honorable course. An honorable person. 2 [for mal] nin wada shukaansi guur-doon ah. e.g. His honor able intentions. 3 Honorable, magac-xurmeed lasiiyo garsoorayaal ama madax-sare. -honorableness n.; - honorably adv.

honorable discharge n. hawl ciidameed oo sharaf looga tago. e.g. The major received an honorable discharge from the army.

honorable mention n. abaalmarin ah xushmo iyo qaddarin. honorand (‘aanarandh) n. la mid honoree.

honorarium (,aana’reeriiyam) n., pl. honorariums or hono raria. lacag hawlqabad ahaan loo siiyo xeeldheerayaal. honorary (‘aana,reeri) adj. 1 loo bixiyay mudnaan. e.g. An honorary degree. 2 qof haya xil ama magac lagu maamuusay.

honoree (,aana’rii) n. qof mudnaan la siiyo. honor guard n. eray kale oo la mid ah guard of honor. honorific (,aana’rifki) adj. loo siiyay sharaf ahaan; lagu sharfay. -honorifically adv.

honor society n. urur ardo dugsi sare ama kulleejo oo hantay heer waxbarasho sare.

honor system n. hab aamineed, siiba bixin lacag ama dhiibid imtixaan.

hood2 n. [informal] mooryaan; jirri.

-hood dibgale (suffix) 1 tilmaanta xaalad ama goor jirijirtay. e.g. Childhood = waqtigii carruurnimada. 2 tilmaanta koox. e.g. brotherhood.

hooded (‘huudhidh) adj. 1 hagoog leh. 2 hagoogan. e.g. A hooded man. 3 indhaxamil ah. e.g. A tall man with hooded eyes.

-v., hoodooed, hoodooing. 1 sixrid; falid. e.g. She’s hoodooed him. 2 keenid ayaandaro.

hoof (huuf) n., pl. hoofs or hooves (huuviz), qoob, siiba mid gammaaneed ama lo’eed; raaf, siiba mid ariyeed ama ugaareed.

-v. 1 hoof it, lugayn; socotin. 2 qoob-cayaarid. -on the hoof, aan wali la qalin, siiba xoolo. - hoofed adj.

hoof-and-mouth disease n. eray kale ee la mid ah foot and-mouth disease.

hoofer (‘hoofar) n. [informal] qof ku xeeldheer qoobcayaar. hoo-ha (‘huu ,haa) n. [informal] huu-haa; walaahow; keena buuq iyo qaylo.

hook (huuk) n. 1 hangool ama shay kale oo af-qoroofan. 2 fishhook, jillaab; bir af-qaroofan oo lagu dabo kalluun. 3 salka telafoon ee gacanka la saaro. 4 waxyaalo soo jiita qof. 5 qalab wax lagu jaro oo qoolaaban. 6 suxlin, siiba marka la feertamayo. 7 far ama qoraal qalloocan oo lagu far-barto.

1. hook 2. hook

-v. 1 suran; ku laaban. e.g. He arms hooked around hers. 2 qaroofid; ku laabid. 3 qallocmid. e.g. The river hooks sharply to the north here. 4 jillaabid. e.g. He hooked a big fish. 5 [informal] xadid. e.g. He hooked money from the neighbors. 6 jiqilayn; xusulayn, siiba feeryahan.

-by hook or by crook, si kasta oo suurtagal noqon karta.

-get (or give someone) the hook, [informal] siiddayn; shaqo ka eryid.

-off the hook, [informal] a ka fakada dhib ama xil. b telafoon ka-la-qaadan ama aan isa-saarnayn. -hook someone/something up or (hook up), ku xirid qalab koronto. -hookless adj.; -hooklet n.; - hooklike adj.

hookah (‘huuka) n. [also houka] shiishad; tubaako laga dhuuqo dhuun dheer oo dhexmarta weel biyo ku jiraan; badeecad; {hukka}.

hook and eye n. isa-suran; bir-yar oo qaroofan iyo mid ay sumato.

hooked (huukit) adj. 1 af-godan ama qaroofan leh. e.g. Hooked earrings. 2 sida hangool u-godan. e.g. A bird with hooked beak. 3 qabatimay. e.g. A Somali teenage boy who got hooked on jaad. 4 ku-xirmay. e.g. She hooked on television.

hooker (‘huukar) n. [informal] dhillo; sharmuuto. hook-nosed adj. sanqaroor qalloocan leh.
